6. IMO environmental compliance - CII ratings, MARPOL

10. Environmental litigation - LA air quality lawsuit, bunker spill

This is clearly a **COMPLEX** query requiring a research plan and multiple specialists. The user has provided extensive detail about the transaction, which means this is a comprehensive due diligence memorandum request.

- Multiple entities: Acquirer (Global Logistics Partners), Target (PMSC), multiple regulatory agencies
